Academy of Astronautics">\n         International Academy of Astronautics\n        </a>\n        (1966)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Klement_Gottwald" title="Order of Klement Gottwald">\n         Order of Klement Gottwald\n        </a>\n        (Czechoslovak Socialist Republic)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Jubilee_Medal_%2250_Years_of_the_Armed_Forces_of_the_USSR%22" title=\'Jubilee Medal "50 Years of the Armed Forces of the USSR"\'>\n         Jubilee Medal "50 Years of the Armed Forces of the USSR"\n        </a>\n        (USSR, January 1968)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Konstantin Tsiolkovsky Gold Medal "for outstanding work in the field of interplanetary communications" (USSR)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Medal of de Lavaux (FAI)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Gold medal and diploma "Man in Space", the Italian Association of Space\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Gold Medal "For outstanding difference" and the Royal Aero Club Diploma,\n        <a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">\n         Sweden\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Medal of Columbus (Italy)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Gold Medal of Saint-Denis (France)\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Gold Medal Award "for courage" of the Fund Matstsotti (Italy), 2007\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p>\n       and others.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Yuri Gagarin was elected an honorary citizen of the following cities:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USSR" title="USSR">\n         USSR\n        </a>\n        :\n        <a href="/wiki/Kaluga" title="Kaluga">\n         Kaluga\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Novozybkov" title="Novozybkov">\n         Novozybkov\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Klintsy" title="Klintsy">\n         Klintsy\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Novocherkassk" title="Novocherkassk">\n         Novocherkassk\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Lyubertsy" title="Lyubertsy">\n         Lyubertsy\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Sumqayit" title="Sumqayit">\n         Sumqayit\n        </a>\n        (in modern-day\n        <a href="/wiki/Azerbaijan" title="Azerbaijan">\n         Azerbaijan\n        </a>\n        ),\n        <a href="/wiki/Smolensk" title="Smolensk">\n         Smolensk\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Vinnytsia" title="Vinnytsia">\n         Vinnytsia\n        </a>\n        (in modern-day\n        <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">\n         Ukraine\n        </a>\n        ),\n        <a href="/wiki/Sevastopol" title="Sevastopol">\n         Sevastopol\n        </a>\n        (in\n        <a href="/wiki/Crimea" title="Crimea">\n         Crimea\n        </a>\n        ),\n        <a href="/wiki/Saratov" title="Saratov">\n         Saratov\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Komsomolsk-on-Amur" title="Komsomolsk-on-Amur">\n         Komsomolsk-on-Amur\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Tyumen" title="Tyumen">\n         Tyumen\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Russia:\n        <a href="/wiki/Orenburg" title="Orenburg">\n         Orenburg\n        </a>\n        <sup class="reference"       </a>\n        :\n        <a href="/wiki/Sofia" title="Sofia">\n         Sofia\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Pernik" title="Pernik">\n         Pernik\n        </a>\n        ,\n      <a href="/wiki/Athens" title="Athens">\n         Athens\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Cyprus" title="Cyprus">\n         Cyprus\n        </a>\n        :\n        <a href="/wiki/Famagusta" title="Famagusta">\n         Famagusta\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Limassol" title="Limassol">\n         Limassol\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        France:\n        <a href="/wiki/Saint-Denis,_Seine-Saint-Denis" title="Saint-Denis, Seine-Saint-Denis">\n         Saint-Denis\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a Tren\xc4\x8dianske Teplice\n        </a>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p>\n       He was also awarded the golden keys to the gates of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">\n        Egyptian\n       </a>\n       cities\n       <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">\n        Cairo\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Alexandria" title="Alexandria">\n        Alexandria\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">\n        See also\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div aria-label="Portals" class="noprint metadata
